```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result

def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```
